Abstract: We propose a feature-based reduced-order model to predict the transient dynamics of bluff-body wakes under arbitrary time-varying actuation. Starting point is a control-oriented POD Galerkin modeling which is challenged by incorporating time-varying actuations as a free input. Our model includes three key enablers. First, POD modes are replaced by a more accurate feature-based manifold of same dimension. Second, a state space is distilled from dynamic features which encapsulate time-varying coherent structures. Third, this state space is augmented for the transient actuation response. Thus, a simple analytical manifold dynamics is obtained. The approach is applied to the fluidic pinball at Re=30, a canonical configuration of three identical circular cylinders arranged in an equilateral triangle and immersed in uniform flow under symmetric actuation. The model is validated against several representative actuation scenarios and accurately reproduces the transient dynamics without requiring unsteady training data, providing an interpretable, observable-based and control-oriented framework. ### [120] [Why gas-focused microjets are so fast: kinetically resolved, shear-driven flow focusing in vacuum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11802)
*Alfonso M. Ganan-Calvo*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用确定性动力学求解器（Shakhov-BGK方程）解析气体膨胀过程，并将其与细长液体射流耦合计算。

Result: 射流速度异常的原因是剪切驱动而非压力驱动：高超音速气体的切向应力提供了几乎全部轴向动量。气体在近场后并未进入弹道区，其应力呈幂律衰减并保持耦合。通过热力学Deborah数Deθ≈Kn·M（Knudsen数×马赫数）统一描述气体本构状态，Deθ=1曲面标定了牛顿气体闭合失效的边界，对应小δ（δ=D/ℓ₀）的真空区域。

Conclusion: 揭示了气体聚焦微射流的物理机制为剪切驱动，建立了稀薄气体动力学与射流耦合的理论框架，动力学计算的表面应力可作为后续非牛顿（粘弹性）液体分析的输入条件。

Abstract: Gas-focused liquid microjets -- the flow-focusing sample delivery on which serial femtosecond crystallography depends -- reach speeds several times the pressure-driven (Bernoulli) bound, unexplained by continuum, local-equilibrium models that do not resolve the rarefied, hypersonic expansion of the focusing gas. We resolve that expansion with a deterministic kinetic (Shakhov--BGK) solver and couple it to the slender liquid jet. The jet is \emph{shear-driven}, not pressure-driven: the tangential stress of the hypersonic gas supplies nearly all of the axial momentum, accounting for the anomalous speed. The gas does not become ballistic behind the near field -- its stress decays as a power law and it stays coupled -- and its constitutive regime is set by a single rarefaction parameter $δ=D/\ell_0$, the orifice diameter over the source mean free path, through the thermodynamic Deborah number $De_θ\simeq K\!n\,M$ (Knudsen times Mach), whose $De_θ=1$ surface maps where the Newtonian-gas closure fails: the small-$δ$ vacuum corner where crystallography jets operate. The kinetically computed surface stress is the input for the fully non-Newtonian (viscoelastic-liquid) sequel.

### [121] [Coherence as Thermodynamic Organization: Toward a Non-Equilibrium Turbulence Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11817)
*Sharath S. Girimaji*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

Conclusion: 该范式为非平衡理论奠定了严格基础，能够明确识别连续驱动、耗散连续系统中所需的流动解析度。

Abstract: Since the foundational studies in the late nineteenth century, fluid turbulence has stood as a profound, unsolved challenge in classical physics. Much of this enduring difficulty stems from non-equilibrium turbulence, where the lack of a unifying physical framework for macroscopic coherent structures has hampered predictive flow modeling. Here, we establish a foundational bridge between non-equilibrium statistical physics and turbulent coherent structures through the renormalized Navier-Stokes equations. We demonstrate that all forms of turbulent coherence are fundamentally universal thermodynamic responses mandated by macroscopic energy throughput imbalances. Depending on topological access to bifurcations, these formations manifest either as transient adjustments (analogous to Kubo's near-equilibrium fluctuations) or as autonomous, transformative states (mirroring Prigogine's far-from-equilibrium dissipative structures). By introducing a computable, effective thermodynamic order parameter ($Π$), this paradigm establishes a rigorous foundation for non-equilibrium theory, enabling unequivocal identification of necessary flow resolution in continuously driven, dissipative continuum systems.

</details>

### [122] [Accessing 100 GHz Mechanical Modes in Bulk Crystals at Cryogenic Temperatures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10737)
*Boxuan Tian,Jiacheng Xie,Hong X. Tang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用即插即用的三维微波腔体（频率可调的超导铌腔）耦合体块铌酸锂晶体，在4 K温度下实现7.0–110 GHz频率范围内厘米尺度、毫克质量机械振动模式的非接触激发与检测；通过测量机械品质因子（W波段达30,000）和微波-声子协同性（最高16.6@110 GHz）来表征耦合强度。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一个通用平台，可获取大质量（厘米尺度、毫克质量）高频机械模式，为在实验友好的开尔文温度下进行机械量子物理的高精度测试铺平了道路，拓展了体块晶体在亚太赫兹电机械学中的应用前景。

Abstract: Sub-terahertz electromechanics offers a promising route to probe mechanical quantum motion at experimentally friendly Kelvin temperatures. Traditionally, high-frequency mechanical resonators rely on advanced microfabrication to shape complex microstructures, while bulk crystals have been largely overlooked due to their large inertia and challenging transduction at such frequencies. Here we show that bulk lithium niobate can host mechanically accessible modes near 100 GHz when coupled via plug-and-play three-dimensional microwave cavities. This approach enables efficient, non-contact excitation of centimeter-scale, milligram-mass vibrational modes across 7.0--110 GHz, with mechanical quality factors up to 30,000 at W band. Furthermore, using a frequency-tunable superconducting niobium cavity at 4 K, we demonstrate strong coupling between a microwave cavity mode and multiple mechanical modes, enabling coherent energy exchange between microwave photons and mechanical phonons with cooperativity up to 16.6 at 110 GHz. These results establish a versatile platform for accessing massive high-frequency mechanical modes and for precision tests of mechanical quantum physics at elevated temperatures.

### [123] [SpectraSensML Software: Mastering Complete Spectral Information for Luminescence Thermometry 2.0](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10807)
*Aleksandar Ćirić,Zoran Ristić,Tamara Gavrilović,Anđela Rajčić,Snežana Đurković,Željka Antić,Miroslav D. Dramićanin*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出发光测温学2.0（LT 2.0）范式，通过SpectraSensML平台对完整发射光谱进行机器学习回归分析，在Yb3+掺杂荧光粉上实现了0.36 K的RMSE，较传统发光强度比方法提升七倍，并揭示了单组分方法的次优性及决策树集成的外推失败机理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统发光测温方法仅利用光谱中少量预选特征（如发光强度比、带宽、线移、激发态寿命），而绝大部分蕴含温度信息的完整光谱数据被系统性丢弃，这种信息利用方式存在根本性局限。

Method: 提出发光测温学2.0范式，基于新开发的SpectraSensML平台，对完整发射光谱施加机器学习回归；在125–700 K范围内对Yb3+掺杂近红外荧光粉进行实验验证；系统比较了四个家族（树集成、物理感知回归、核与实例方法、神经网络）的19种回归算法；采用传感器融合估计器结合前三个主成分。

Result: 传感器融合估计器达到0.36 K的RMSE，较最佳发光强度比方法提升七倍；多组分回归器利用前三个主成分可将温度不确定性降低近一个数量级；发现决策树集成在未见温度点上因分段常数预测无法插值而失败。

Conclusion: 全光谱机器学习回归范式（LT 2.0）显著优于传统单特征方法，开源SpectraSensML平台可复现基准测试结果，为发光测温领域提供了新方向。

Abstract: Luminescence thermometry has evolved through decades of research focused on optimising materials and on extracting temperature information from isolated spectral features such as luminescence intensity ratios, bandwidth, line shift and excited-state lifetime. Despite extensive material development, these conventional methods remain fundamentally limited by construction: only a small subset of pre-selected spectral features is exploited, while the bulk of the temperature-relevant information encoded in the full spectrum is systematically discarded. A paradigm shift is presented here, Luminescence Thermometry 2.0 (LT 2.0), implemented through the newly developed SpectraSensML platform, in which machine learning regression operates on the entire emission spectrum to deliver temperature readout. The approach is demonstrated on a Yb3+-doped phosphor emitting in the near-infrared biological transparency window across 125 to 700 K. Nineteen regression algorithms drawn from four families, namely tree ensembles, physics-aware regression models, kernel and instance methods, and neural networks, are systematically benchmarked. A sensor-fusion estimator that combines the first three principal components reaches an root-mean-square error of 0.36 K, a seven-fold improvement over the best luminescence intensity ratio variant. Single-component approaches are shown to be quantitatively sub-optimal: multi-component regressors that exploit the first three principal components reduce the temperature uncertainty by close to an order of magnitude. The structural reason behind the failure of decision-tree ensembles on unseen temperatures is explained: their piecewise-constant predictions cannot interpolate beyond training set-points. The open-source SpectraSensML application used to obtain the results is released alongside the manuscript to enable reproducible community benchmarks.

</details>


### [124] [Multiple Band-Gaps through the Coupling of Unit Cells from the Same Metamaterial: the Dual Cell method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10916)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索通过将同种力学超材料的两个单胞耦合为双胞构型，能否产生具有更强波动衰减能力的新型超材料，并验证"任何带隙超材料都存在由其自身单胞构建的更高效版本"这一设想。

Method: 在2D空间中研究两种耦合配置（并排和棋盘格），保持高对称性平面晶体群以简化能带计算；同时在1D弹簧质量链上应用相同方法揭示带隙涌现机制。

Result: 特定配置和单胞选择下，出现了多个方向性和/或全向带隙，其中部分带隙展现出增强的衰减效果。

Conclusion: 任何带隙超材料都可以通过将其自身单胞进行特定耦合，构建出波动衰减能力更强的版本。

Abstract: This study investigates how the coupling of two unit cells belonging to the same mechanical metamaterial into a dual unit cell configuration, can produce a new metamaterial with enhanced wave attenuation capabilities. For two metamaterials, two different unit cell coupling configurations are examined in 2D (side by side and chessboard), with particular emphasis on maintaining a plane crystallographic group of high symmetry, in order to simplify band structure calculations given the complexity of the geometry. It is shown that for specific configurations and choices of unit cell, multiple directional and/or omnidirectional band-gaps can appear, some of which can exhibit enhanced attenuation. The way in which these band-gaps emerge is described through applying the same procedure on 1D spring mass chains. Results support the idea that any band-gap metamaterial could have a much more efficient version which can be constructed purely from its own unit cells.

### [125] [What You Train Is What You Get: Gender Bias, Training Composition, and Post-Hoc Mitigation in Audio Deepfake Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09891)
*Aishwarya R. Fursule,Vamshi Nallaguntla,Shruti Kshirsagar,Anderson R. Avila*

Main category: cs.SD

TL;DR: 本研究在ASVspoof5数据集上系统性地探究了音频深度伪造检测中的性别偏差问题，发现训练数据的性别组成强烈预测偏差方向，WavLM特征比LogSpectrogram放大3.0-4.3倍的性别性能差距，且六种后验阈值校准方法均无法纠正底层分数分布的不均衡（EER差距稳定在1.317个百分点），表明性别公平性必须在训练阶段解决。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有音频深度伪造检测模型虽然总体准确率高，但可能掩盖不同人口群体间的显著性能差异，本研究旨在系统性地探究性别偏差的存在性、成因及可能的缓解手段。

Method: 使用ASVspoof5数据集构建受控的自定义划分以隔离性别组成效应，训练9种不同性别组成（从全女性到全男性）训练集上的攻击特定模型，采用ResNet18分类器搭配LogSpectrogram和WavLM-Base+两种特征，并评估六种后验阈值校准方法。

Result: 训练数据性别组成强烈预测偏差方向，少数性别在测试时性能更差；WavLM特征产生的性别性能差距是LogSpectrogram的3.0-4.3倍；平衡训练可减少LogSpectrogram偏差但对WavLM效果有限；六种校准策略均无法改变EER差距（固定为1.317个百分点）。

Conclusion: 音频深度伪造检测中的性别公平性必须在训练阶段解决，后验方法只能部分缓解由此产生的差异。

Abstract: Audio deepfake detection models determine whether speech is genuine or artificially generated, but high overall accuracy can mask substantial performance disparities across demographic groups. In this work, we investigate gender bias in audio deepfake detection using the ASVspoof5 dataset. We use ASVspoof5 under a controlled custom split designed to isolate gender-composition effects. We train attack-specific models on nine training sets with different gender compositions, ranging from female-only to male-only. We use a ResNet18 classifier with LogSpectrogram and WavLM-Base+ features, and we evaluated six post-hoc threshold calibration methods. Experimental results show that training data composition strongly predicts bias direction, with the underrepresented gender performing worse at test time. WavLM-Base+ features are shown to produce gender performance gaps 3.0 to 4.3 times larger than LogSpectrogram under identical training conditions, and balanced training is found to reduce LogSpectrogram bias but leave WavLM bias largely intact. Moreover, all six calibration strategies, including Oracle calibration with full test-set label access, leave the Equal Error Rate gap unchanged at 1.317 pp, confirming that threshold adjustment cannot correct underlying score distribution disparities. Overall, these findings suggest that gender fairness in audio deepfake detection must be addressed at training time, as post-hoc methods can only partially mitigate the resulting disparities

### [126] [A Production-Oriented Framework for Evaluation of SFX Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09973)
*Mélodie Desbos,Yara Bahram,Eric Granger,Mohammadhadi Shateri*

Main category: cs.SD

TL;DR: 本文提出了一套面向工业音效设计的评估框架，用于结构化比较异构音频生成与编辑方法。框架定义了9项生产需求，引入两阶段评估协议（参考引导的音频到音频变异任务+能力特定分析），结合客观指标（FAD、ImageBind参考对齐、多样性）和人类研究（感知身份保持、瞬态诊断）。实验揭示了不同基线方法在参考对齐与多样性之间的互补优势与权衡，其中AudioX在共享ATA设置下表现最佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有音效生成评估通常绑定到文本到音频、无条件或特定任务场景，缺乏对参考引导的音效变体生成的结构化评估，无法满足工业音效设计对真实感、感知身份保持、可控变化和高效工作流的需求。

Method: 提出生产导向评估框架：1）识别9项生产需求；2）两阶段协议——阶段一为参考引导的音频到音频变异任务（基于ESC-50 SFX适配设置统一评估），阶段二为能力特定分析（涵盖SFX变形、时间与能量对齐、修补、目标编辑）；3）结合客观指标（FAD、ImageBind参考对齐、多样性）和人类研究（感知身份保持、瞬态诊断）。

Result: 不同基线在参考对齐与多样性间存在互补优势与权衡。在共享ATA设置下，AudioX在参考对齐与多样性之间提供了最强的整体平衡，同时支持SFX变形；其他基线在特定编辑操作上表现更优。

Conclusion: 该框架为参考引导的SFX变体建立了结构化评估与决策协议，为设计未来统一的工业音频生成流水线提供了实用基础。

Abstract: Industrial sound design requires audio generation systems that not only produce realistic audio, but also preserve the perceptual identity of a reference, support controllable variation, and remain efficient for practical workflows. Existing evaluations are usually tied to text-to-audio (TTA), unconditional, or task-specific settings, limiting assessment for reference-guided sound effects (SFX) variation. To address this gap, we present a production-oriented evaluation framework for structured comparison of heterogeneous audio generation and editing methods. Our framework identifies nine production requirements and explicitly accounts for differences in model capabilities, enabling comparison under a common production objective. A two-stage protocol is introduced: (1) a reference-guided audio-to-audio (ATA) variation task, in which all methods are evaluated under the same ESC-50 SFX adaptation setup, and (2) capability-specific analyses of native operations such as SFX morphing, temporal and energy alignment, inpainting, and targeted editing. This framework combines objective metrics (including FAD, ImageBind-based reference alignment, and diversity across generated variants), together with a human study of perceptual identity preservation and transient diagnosis. Our study reveals complementary strengths and trade-offs across baselines for different production needs. Among the full-generation baselines evaluated under a shared ATA setting, AudioX provides the strongest overall trade-off between reference alignment and diversity while still supporting SFX morphing. Other baselines remain most suitable for specific editing operations. Our framework establishes a structured evaluation and decision protocol for reference-guided SFX variation and provides a practical basis for designing future unified industrial audio generation pipelines. Audio demos are on the accompanying web page.

### [127] [ARIMA: Reconstruction-Grounded Predictive Representation Learning for Symbolic Music](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10003)
*Mingyang Yao,Zhaoxiang Feng*

Main category: cs.SD

TL;DR: 本文提出ARIMA，一种基于重建引导的潜在预测框架，用于符号音乐的自监督学习，通过编码固定时长窗口为连续潜在表示、对比性下一潜在预测和结构化重建，在保留局部音乐细节的同时建模时间进展。实验表明ARIMA在和声、时序及跨演奏检索任务上高效且有效，消融实验验证了下一潜在预测和结构化重建的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有符号音乐的自监督学习主要依赖token级别的预训练，但这类表示受限于分词器特定的序列，且通常只能间接提供时间跨度级别的嵌入。ARIMA旨在学习直接从数据中获取紧凑的窗口化表示，以克服上述局限性。

Method: ARIMA包含三个核心设计：(1) 将每个固定时长的音乐窗口编码为连续潜在表示；(2) 使用对比性下一潜在预测训练因果预测器；(3) 通过音乐元素的结构化重建对编码器进行约束。该方法在保留局部音乐细节的同时对跨窗口的时间进展进行建模。

Result: ARIMA在和声、时序及跨演奏检索等下游任务上表现出高效性和有效性，在其它任务上与更大的基线模型具有竞争力。消融实验表明下一潜在预测对获得时间整合表示至关重要，结构化重建能够稳定潜在学习且无需显式方差正则化。

Conclusion: ARIMA作为一种重建引导的潜在预测框架，为符号音乐学习提供了一种不依赖token级预训练的新范式，在多项音乐理解任务上展现出优异的效率与效果。

Abstract: Self-supervised learning for symbolic music has advanced largely through token-level pretraining, but such representations remain tied to tokenizer-specific sequences and often provide time-span-level embeddings only indirectly. In this paper, we propose ARIMA, a reconstruction-grounded latent predictive framework for symbolic music that learns compact window-based representations directly from data. ARIMA encodes each fixed-duration window into a continuous latent representation, trains a causal predictor with contrastive next-latent prediction, and grounds the encoder through structured reconstruction of music elements. This design preserves local musical details while modeling temporal progression across windows. We evaluate ARIMA on downstream tasks spanning various levels of music understanding. Results show that ARIMA is particularly efficient and effective on tasks involving harmonic, timing, and cross-performance retrieval, while remaining competitive with much larger baselines on other tasks. Ablations further show that next-latent prediction is essential for temporally integrated representations, and that structured reconstruction stabilizes latent learning without requiring explicit variance regularization. The code is at https://github.com/AndyWeasley2004/symbolic_music_wm.

</details>


### [128] [Local Multimodal Music Alignment from Global Supervision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10023)
*Irmak Bukey,Zachary Novack,Jongmin Jung,Dasaem Jeong,Chris Donahue*

Main category: cs.SD

TL;DR: 提出FuSiLi，一种基于Sinkhorn软对齐的多模态对比学习相似度评分，仅需全局监督即可学习音视频局部对应关系，在乐谱图像与音频的局部对齐任务上优于现有方法，同时保持全局检索能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 音乐理解需要跨模态的局部对应关系（如音频时间点与乐谱图像位置的映射），但局部对应关系的监督信号难以获取，实践中通常只有全局层面的监督信号（如成对的音频与图像片段）。

Method: 提出FuSiLi（Fused Sinkhorn-Localized Similarity），通过Sinkhorn算法对局部图像块特征和音频帧特征进行软对齐，结合传统全局相似度构建混合对比学习目标，微调预训练的CLIP和CLAP编码器。

Result: 在跨模态检索和帧级对齐任务上，与多种全局和局部基线方法对比，FuSiLi在局部对齐任务上表现更优，同时在检索任务上保持竞争力。

Conclusion: FuSiLi有效学习了局部跨模态对应关系，仅需全局监督即可实现，且不牺牲全局对齐能力。

Abstract: Understanding music requires understanding localized relationships across data modalities, e.g., how time in performance audio maps onto position in a score image. Yet supervision for such local correspondences is difficult to obtain-in practice, we often only have access to coarser global supervision like paired segments of audio and images. To address this gap, we propose FuSiLi (Fused Sinkhorn-Localized Similarity), a similarity score for multimodal contrastive learning operating directly on local image patch and audio frame features via Sinkhorn-based soft alignment. We show that FuSiLi (i) effectively learns local relationships, (ii) requires only global supervision, and (iii) retains the global alignment capabilities of conventional contrastive approaches. We fine-tune pretrained CLIP and CLAP encoders on pairs of raw sheet music images and audio using a hybrid contrastive objective combining FuSiLi with conventional global similarity. We evaluate on cross-modal retrieval and frame-level alignment tasks against a range of global and local baselines, showing that our approach outperforms them on local alignment while remaining competitive on retrieval.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 阿尔茨海默症早期发现困难，神经影像成本高，基于语言的工具在资源受限场景下不可用；现有自发语音方法多依赖转录/ASR或计算密集型深度模型，缺乏简单、音频-only的基线方案。

Method: 使用 DementiaBank Pitt 语料库中176份Cookie Theft录音（88 AD/88 对照）；采用WebRTC VAD分离语音与非语音；提取99个手工声学-时间特征（停顿与流利度统计、频谱/韵律描述符、MFCC及其Δ和ΔΔ摘要）；使用GroupShuffleSplit进行说话人独立评估，30次迭代；分类器为轻量级RBF核SVM。

Result: RBF-SVM在30次迭代中平均AUC为0.674；单次分割可达AUC 0.742、准确率0.657；基于Random Forest重要性的Top-20特征子集AUC为0.719（但未嵌套在训练分割中，结论偏乐观，不作为主要结论）。

Conclusion: 免转录的频谱-时间与流利度线索可在说话人独立条件下从原始音频实现AD筛查，为面向部署的研究提供了实用基础。

Abstract: It is still hard to find Alzheimer's disease (AD) early, especially when neuroimaging is expensive or tools that depend on language are not available. Spontaneous speech provides a non-invasive signal; however, numerous current methodologies depend on transcripts/ASR or computationally intensive deep models. We offer a simple, audio-only baseline for detecting AD using 176 Cookie Theft recordings from the DementiaBank Pitt corpus (88 AD, 88 controls). WebRTC voice activity detection (VAD) is used to separate speech from non-speech. We take out 99 hand-crafted acoustic-temporal features, including pause and fluency statistics, spectral/prosodic descriptors, and MFCC summaries with Δ and ΔΔ. Evaluation is performed using a stringent speaker-independent GroupShuffleSplit,documenting performance across 30 iterations. A lightweight SVM with an RBF kernel gets an average AUC of 0.674 across runs. For example, a single split has an AUC of 0.742 and an accuracy of 0.657. We also present an exploratory compact-feature analysis utilizing a Top-20 subset ranked by Random Forest importance; since selection is not nested within training splits, these results may be overly optimistic and are not employed for primary conclusions (AUC 0.719). The results indicate that transcript-free spectro-temporal and fluency-related cues can facilitate speaker-independent Alzheimer's disease screening from raw audio, establishing a practical foundation for deployment-oriented research.

### [130] [Breaking the Quality--Intelligibility Trade-off in Streaming Target Speaker Extraction via Deep-Feature-Anchored Preference Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10191)
*Shuhai Peng,Jinjiang Liu,Hui Lu,Liyang Chen,Guiping Zhong,Jiakui Li,Shiyin Kang,Zhiyong Wu*

Main category: cs.SD

TL;DR: 本文揭示了生成式流式目标说话人提取（TSE）中质量-可懂度权衡的根本原因在于优化锚点选择不当而非流式架构限制，并提出WavLM锚定的直接偏好优化（DPO）微调策略和扩大Conformer卷积核两种互补改进，在560ms流式块大小下实现了10.9%的相对可懂度提升（WER从0.138降至0.123），同时音频质量和说话人相似度略有改善。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式流式TSE模型存在质量-可懂度权衡问题，直接优化音频质量指标会导致灾难性奖励破解（catastrophic reward hacking），系统性地擦除对发音和可懂度至关重要的内容。作者揭示该权衡的根本原因在于优化锚点选择不当，而非流式架构的限制。

Method: 提出两种互补改进：（1）扩大Conformer卷积核以增强局部时频建模能力；（2）基于WavLM的DPO微调策略，其中偏好对由WavLM余弦相似度排序，该深度声学特征编码了音系结构和说话人身份，提供抗破解的优化锚点。

Result: 在560ms流式块大小下，WER从0.138降至0.123（相对改善10.9%），同时音频质量和说话人相似度获得边际提升。

Conclusion: 质量-可懂度权衡并非流式架构固有，可通过合适的优化锚点（如WavLM）和架构改进（扩大卷积核）有效突破。

Abstract: Generative streaming models for Target Speaker Extraction (TSE) commonly exhibit a quality--intelligibility trade-off, wherein naive optimization for perceptual audio quality tends to degrade speech intelligibility, and conversely. We reveal that this trade-off arises not from the constraints of streaming architectures, but from an inappropriate choice of optimization anchor. Directly optimizing against audio quality metrics induces catastrophic reward hacking, where content critical to pronunciation and intelligibility is systematically erased to maximize a proxy score. To break this bottleneck, we propose two complementary improvements: an enlarged Conformer convolution kernel for richer local spectro-temporal modeling, and WavLM-anchored Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) fine-tuning strategy. DPO preference pairs are ranked by WavLM cosine similarity, a deep acoustic feature encoding both phonetic structure and speaker identity, providing an optimization anchor that resists hacking. Under a 560 ms streaming chunk size, the proposed method achieves a 10.9% relative intelligibility improvement (word error rate: 0.138 to 0.123), with marginal simultaneous gains in audio quality and speaker similarity.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖手工规则或基于启发式/程序化生成伪标签的显著性分类器，存在生成器偏差且无法显式优化连贯的简化旋律。

Method: 提出MeloBottleneck框架，包含硬瓶颈提取器（选择音符事件）、节奏闭合算子（生成自洽骨架）、重装饰解码器（重构输入旋律），结合重构损失、冻结自回归旋律先验、装饰不变一致性及装饰排除进行自监督训练。

Abstract: Melody skeleton extraction aims to derive a shorter melody that preserves structural notes while removing ornaments. Prior methods rely on hand-crafted reduction rules or note-wise salience classifiers trained with heuristically or procedurally generated pseudo-labels. Such supervision can inherit generator bias and does not explicitly optimize a coherent reduced melody. We introduce MeloBottleneck, a self-supervised framework that represents a skeleton as a length-controlled, order-preserving latent subsequence. A hard-bottleneck extractor selects note events, a rhythmic-closure operator produces a self-consistent skeleton, and a re-ornamentation decoder reconstructs the input melody. Training combines reconstruction, a frozen autoregressive melody prior, ornament-invariant consistency across procedurally ornamented views, and ornament exclusion. We evaluate three regimes: synthetic out-of-distribution ornament-to-skeleton, TAVERN variation-to-theme, and Jiugong ornamented-to-gongche. A matched pseudo-label classifier excels on the synthetic benchmark, while MeloBottleneck transfers better, achieving competitive selection quality on TAVERN and Jiugong. Skeletonized melodies also improve BM25-based fragment retrieval, boosting Recall@K and MRR while reducing query time. Overall, the results suggest that learning skeletons as latent subsequences yields more robust transfer than pseudo-label imitation.

This design addresses two major gaps in existing partial spoofing benchmarks: the lack of realistic environmental sounds in speech partial spoofing scenarios and the absence of partial spoofing detection for environmental sound components. We further establish standardized evaluation protocols and design a joint learning framework to optimize spoofing detection across speech, environmental sound, and mixed audio. The results demonstrate that training under matched target conditions is more effective than directly transferring models trained on speech or environmental sound components.

### [136] [CHARM: Charge Calibration and Acoustic Rescue for LLM-based Multimodal Sarcasm Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11102)
*Qiyang Sun,Yi Chang,Yupei Li,Xi Shao,Zixing Zhang,Björn W. Schuller*

TL;DR: 提出CHARM框架，通过双向电荷校准（BiCAL）和声学后融合救援（ALFR）两个模块，在不微调的情况下实现零样本多模态讽刺检测，在MUStARD和CMMA数据集上取得了SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 零样本指令微调大语言模型在讽刺检测中系统性地过度预测正面（讽刺）类别，且人类依赖的韵律线索未被充分利用并在语言间迁移不均。

Method: BiCAL通过对称轴上的电荷提示引导LLM产生相反的讽刺和字面判决，消除方向性偏差后聚合得到无偏语用信号；ALFR将校准后的文本投票与韵律描述符及LLM生成的听觉感知探针通过浅层分类器融合，主动降低饱和文本投票权重以增强声学证据。

Result: BiCAL在MUStARD上零样本文本Macro-F1达0.787，ALFR在CMMA上提升弱骨干网络最多+0.382 Macro-F1。Stouffer元分析验证统计显著性（MUStARD: Z=13.89, CMMA: Z=34.64, p<10^-43）。

Abstract: Sarcasm detection, the identification of discrepancies between literal and intended meaning, is a fundamental task in affective computing. However, zero-shot instruction-tuned Large Language Models (LLMs) systematically over-predict the positive (sarcastic) class across the entire capability spectrum, while the prosodic cues humans rely on remain underexploited and transfer unevenly across languages. We introduce CHARM (Charge Calibration and Acoustic Rescue for Multimodal Sarcasm Detection), a training-free framework that couples two modules. Bidirectional Charge Calibration (BiCAL) steers the LLM toward opposing sarcastic and literal verdicts along a symmetric axis of charged prompts; the induced directional biases cancel by construction, and a simple aggregation recovers an unbiased pragmatic signal. Acoustic Late-Fusion Rescue (ALFR) then fuses the calibrated votes with prosodic descriptors and LLM-generated auditory-perception probes through a shallow classifier, actively down-weighting saturated text votes in favour of acoustic evidence. Without fine-tuning any backbone, BiCAL attains the highest reported zero-shot text-only Macro-F1 of 0.787 on MUStARD, while ALFR lifts weak backbones by up to +0.382 Macro-F1 on CMMA. A Stouffer meta-analysis confirms statistical significance on MUStARD and CMMA (Z = 13.89 and Z = 34.64, respectively; p < 10^-43). Our analysis further uncovers a cross-cultural prosodic decoupling: low-level acoustics fail to transfer across languages, whereas high-level perceptual abstractions remain robust. Together, these components yield an explainable, cross-lingual multimodal detector.

### [137] [MusicMark: A Robust Generative Watermarking Framework for Music Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11117)
*Seohwan Yun,Jeeyoung Yun,Yongjin Kim,Juyeon Lee,Sungwoong Kim*

Main category: cs.SD

TL;DR: MusicMark是首个面向音乐的生成式水印框架，通过在扩散模型的语义潜空间中嵌入水印，使其作为音乐内容的一部分，显著提升了鲁棒性，尤其在应对神经编解码器重合成攻击方面优于后处理方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有音频水印方法主要针对语音，直接应用于音乐时效果不佳；后处理水印方法脆弱易受攻击，且生成与水印解耦导致水印可被绕过，无法提供可靠的来源保障。

Method: 在扩散生成模型中引入水印适配器，在去噪步骤中将水印消息嵌入语义潜空间；适配器和检测器通过联合目标训练，约束水印潜变量接近无水印参考变量以保持保真度，同时通过攻击增强提升鲁棒性。

Result: MusicMark在多种攻击（包括神经编解码器重合成）下显著优于后处理基线方法，同时保持可比的生成质量；在引入的翻唱歌曲攻击中，MusicMark的鲁棒性也优于后处理方法。

Conclusion: 将水印嵌入生成过程中比后处理加水印更具鲁棒性，MusicMark为音乐生成模型的可信来源归属和溯源提供了有效方案。

Abstract: AI music generation has rapidly advanced alongside commercial platforms, raising the need for reliable watermarking for provenance and attribution. However, existing audio watermarking research has largely focused on speech, and applying speech-oriented methods to music is challenging due to music's complex structure and rich acoustic texture. Most existing methods are post-hoc, adding imperceptible perturbations after generation rather than embedding watermarks as part of the content. This makes them fragile under transformations and especially vulnerable to neural codec re-synthesis, which can discard imperceptible residual signals. Moreover, since generation and watermarking are decoupled, the watermarking step can be bypassed or omitted, weakening provenance guarantees. To address these issues, we propose MusicMark, which, to the best of our knowledge, is the first generative watermarking framework for music. Specifically, MusicMark embeds watermark messages into the semantic latent space during generation, incorporating the watermark as part of the musical content and ensuring robustness against diverse attacks, particularly neural codec re-synthesis. To this end, we introduce a watermark adapter into a diffusion-based generation model to embed watermark messages across denoising steps. The adapter and detector are trained with a joint objective that preserves fidelity by constraining watermarked latents close to their unwatermarked reference latents, while improving robustness through attack augmentations. Experiments demonstrate that MusicMark substantially outperforms post-hoc baselines across diverse attacks including neural codec re-synthesis, while maintaining comparable generation quality. We further introduce a cover-song attack, converting the singing voice while preserving musical content, and show that MusicMark remains more robust than post-hoc methods.

</details>


### [138] [BeatEdit: Symbolic Music Generation as Explicit Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11124)
*Haoyu Gu,Lekai Qian,Haowu Zhou,Qi Liu,Shuai Wang*

Main category: cs.SD

TL;DR: 本文提出BeatEdit，首个基于显式编辑操作（而非从头生成）的符号音乐生成框架，通过三种编辑机制（序列标记纠错、迭代精炼伴奏编辑、标记后填充段落补全），在单个预训练骨干网络上实现比自回归和扩散方法更高的精度和感知质量，推理速度低于100ms，并揭示了编码设计对编辑效果的重要影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 音乐创作本质上是修订过程，但现有符号音乐生成范式主要从零开始生成完整序列，缺乏对选择性修改的支持。编辑方法在文本领域效果显著，但在符号音乐中尚未被充分探索，主要原因是传统基于事件的音乐编码缺乏编辑所需的结构特性。

Method: 基于BEAT编码（节拍网格锚定表示），提出BeatEdit框架，包含三种互补机制：1）逐token序列标记用于纠错；2）迭代精炼用于伴奏编辑；3）标签-填充用于段落补全。三者共享同一编码和预训练骨干网络。

Result: 在三个任务上均达到比自回归和扩散方法更高的精度和感知质量，单次推理完成时间低于100ms。跨编码评估表明编码设计显著影响编辑效果，且存在编码-方法交互效应。

Conclusion: BeatEdit首次将显式编辑操作引入符号音乐生成，证明了编辑范式在音乐生成中的有效性，并揭示了音乐编码设计对编辑任务的关键影响。

Abstract: Music creation is fundamentally a process of revision. Yet symbolic music generation remains dominated by paradigms that produce complete sequences from scratch, with limited support for selective modification. Edit-based methods have proven effective for text transformation tasks, but remain largely unexplored for symbolic music. We trace this absence to the representational level: conventional event-based music encodings lack the structural properties required by explicit music editing. In contrast, the BEAT encoding, a beat-grid-anchored representation originally designed for autoregressive generation, possesses structural properties amenable to editing. We propose BeatEdit, the first framework for symbolic music generation based on explicit edit operations, recasting generation as producing new content by editing a draft rather than synthesizing from scratch. BeatEdit comprises three complementary mechanisms along an axis of increasing edit density: per-token sequence tagging for error correction, iterative refinement for accompaniment editing, and tag-then-fill for segment completion. All these mechanisms share a single encoding and pre-trained backbone, achieving higher precision and perceptual quality than autoregressive and diffusion methods across all three tasks, while remaining efficient, with single-pass inference completing in under 100 ms. Cross-encoding evaluation further reveals that encoding design substantially influences editing effectiveness, with notable encoding-method interaction effects. Code is available at https://github.com/Haoyu-Gu/BeatEdit-code

### [139] [Anysynth:Zero-Shot Instrument Cloning via In-Context Learning and Asymmetric Hierarchical Guidance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11143)
*Chong Jing,Junan Zhang,Jing Yang,Yulun Wu,Fan Fan,Zhizheng Wu*

Main category: cs.SD

TL;DR: Anysynth是一种无需嵌入的神经合成器，基于上下文流匹配（in-context flow matching）和扩散Transformer（DiT），通过直接以未压缩的参考音频和目标MIDI为条件，实现零样本乐器克隆，在音频质量、音色相似度和旋律遵循度上超越现有方法，并提出非对称分层CFG优化可控性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有零样本乐器克隆方法依赖预训练嵌入（如CLAP）将参考音频压缩为固定长度向量，丢失了重建音色所需的细粒度声学线索。为此，本文提出无需嵌入的神经合成器，以保留完整声学细节。

Method: 提出Anysynth，基于上下文流匹配的神经合成器。核心是让扩散Transformer（DiT）直接以未压缩的参考音频和目标MIDI序列为条件，通过自注意力机制在生成时动态检索声学细节。此外，提出非对称分层CFG（Asymmetric Hierarchical CFG），解耦MIDI和参考音色的引导，避免梯度冲突。

Result: 在音频质量、音色相似度和旋律遵循度上优于基于嵌入和自回归的基线方法。模型展现出提示长度缩放特性：更长的参考提示持续提升音色保真度，这是嵌入系统不具备的。非对称分层CFG同时提升了音符准确性和音色保真度。

Conclusion: Anysynth通过免嵌入的上下文流匹配框架有效解决了零样本乐器克隆中细粒度声学信息丢失的问题，非对称分层CFG进一步优化了可控性，推动了表达性零样本乐器克隆的发展。

Abstract: Zero-shot instrument cloning aims to render an arbitrary [Target MIDI] sequence with the acoustic identity of an unseen instrument given only a short [Reference Audio, Reference MIDI] pair. Existing methods rely on pre-trained embeddings (e.g., CLAP) that compress the reference audio into a fixed-length vector, discarding fine-grained acoustic cues essential for faithful timbre reconstruction. We present Anysynth, an embedding-free neural synthesizer based on in-context flow matching. By conditioning a Diffusion Transformer (DiT) directly on the uncompressed reference audio and target MIDI, our model allows self-attention to dynamically retrieve acoustic details at generation time. Experiments show that \tool outperforms embedding-based and auto-regressive baselines in audio quality, timbre similarity, and melody adherence. Notably, the model exhibits prompt-length scaling: longer reference prompts yield steadily better timbre fidelity, a property absent in embedding-based systems. To optimize controllability, we further propose Asymmetric Hierarchical CFG, which structurally decouples MIDI and reference-timbre guidance based on their natural semantic-acoustic dependency. This asymmetric formulation avoids gradient conflicts and improves both note accuracy and timbre fidelity, pushing the boundary of expressive, zero-shot instrument cloning. Demo audios are available at https://anysynth-demo.github.io/

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出证据子空间投影方法，在SSL模型神经元激活模式构建的共享空间中，同时表示证据因素（攻击类别、编解码器、性别、传输方式）和真实性标签；通过将决策向量投影到每个证据子空间，获得标量比值来量化各证据类型的解释力。

Result: 在原始、微调、后训练三种设定下、多数据集上评估SSL模型，验证了方法有效性，确认了已有研究结论，并揭示了模型行为的新见解。

Abstract: Self-supervised learning (SSL) models are widely used as feature extractors for state-of-the-art audio deepfake detection, but it remains unclear how to directly and quantitatively connect what SSL models capture to detection decisions. To address this gap, we propose Evidence Subspace Projection, a method that represents both evidence factors (e.g., attack category, codec, gender, transmission) and authenticity labels in a shared space constructed from SSL models' neuron activation patterns. By projecting the decision vector onto each evidence subspace, we obtain a scalar ratio that quantifies the explanatory power of each evidence type. We evaluate SSL models in raw, fine-tuned, and post-trained settings on multiple datasets. The results confirm findings from established studies, validating the proposed method, and reveal new insights into model behavior.

### [141] [Teaching Speech Enhancement Models to Sing: Domain Adaptation from Speech Enhancement to Singing Voice Separation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11630)
*Paul A. Bereuter,Mark D. Plumbley,Alois Sontacchi*

Main category: cs.SD

TL;DR: 本文提出将歌声分离视为从语音增强到歌声分离的域适应问题，研究了全微调和LoRA参数高效微调两种策略。实验表明，两种微调策略均优于从头训练（SDR提升0.29-1.8 dB），全微调分离性能最佳但存在灾难性遗忘，LoRA以仅6-12%的额外参数在保持语音增强能力的同时取得竞争性分离性能，生成模型对未见数据集泛化能力更好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 歌声分离模型受限于可用训练数据不足，而语音增强模型可受益于大规模标注数据集。为克服数据稀缺问题，作者将歌声分离建模为从语音增强到歌声分离的域适应问题。

Method: 采用两种微调策略：全微调和基于LoRA的参数高效微调，分别在判别模型和生成模型上进行实验，将预训练的语音增强模型适配到歌声分离任务。

Result: 两种微调策略均比从头训练高出0.29-1.8 dB（SDR指标）；全微调取得最佳歌声分离性能但导致语音增强性能下降（灾难性遗忘）；LoRA以6-12%额外参数在保持语音增强能力的同时取得竞争性分离性能；生成模型对未见测试集泛化更好。

Conclusion: 适配预训练语音增强模型是数据稀缺场景下训练歌声分离模型的有效策略。

Abstract: State-of-the-art speech enhancement models benefit from large-scale labeled datasets, whereas singing voice separation models suffer from limited available training data. To address this limitation, we formulate singing voice separation as domain adaptation from speech enhancement to singing voice separation. We investigate two fine-tuning strategies: full fine-tuning and parameter-efficient fine-tuning using Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) on a discriminative and a generative model. Models with either adaptation strategy outperform the same architectures trained from scratch by 0.29-1.8 dB in Signal-to-Distortion-Ratio. Full fine-tuning yields the highest singing voice separation performance, but catastrophic forgetting degrades speech enhancement performance. LoRA fine-tuning achieves competitive singing voice separation performance while preserving the original speech enhancement capability with only 6-12% additional parameters compared to the base speech enhancement model. Furthermore, the generative model shows improved generalization to an unseen test set. The results demonstrate that adapting pretrained speech enhancement models is an effective strategy for training singing voice separation models in data-scarce scenarios.

### [142] [Qwen-Music Technical Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11699)
*Jin Xu,Kangdi Wang,Ruibin Yuan,Shun Lei,Xiong Wang,Xize Cheng,Xueyao Zhang,Yang Zhang,Yiheng Chen,Yongqi Wang,Yue Wang,Zhifang Guo,Zihan Liu,Zijian Lin,Dake Guo,Hangrui Hu,Lei Xie,Linhan Ma,Wei Xue,Wenxiang Guo,Xinfa Zhu,Xipin Wei,Yangze Li,Yuanjun Lv,Yuxuan Wang,Yunfei Chu,Zhiyong Wu*

Main category: cs.SD

TL;DR: Qwen-Music是一个强大的音乐生成模型，支持从文本生成音乐和翻唱歌曲生成两种核心任务。它通过三组件架构（Tokenizer、LLM、Render）实现高质量音乐生成，其中Melody-CoT机制通过旋律规划提升音乐性和结构连贯性。模型在超过500万小时多语言数据上训练，采用质量感知预训练课程和渐进式后训练（监督初始化、离线DPO、在线GSPO），在16项客观指标中13项达到SOTA，专业评估者偏好度超越领先商业系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有音乐生成模型在音乐性、保真度、结构连贯性和指令跟随能力上仍有不足，尤其是完整包含人声歌唱的高质量歌曲生成仍具挑战。此外，翻唱歌曲生成中参考旋律的准确保留也是一个待解决的问题。

Method: 采用三组件架构：1) Qwen-Music-Tokenizer将音频压缩为25Hz单码本音乐语义标记；2) Qwen-Music-LLM基于语义标记进行自回归音乐语义建模，核心创新是Melody-CoT机制在完整生成前先规划旋律；3) Qwen-Music-Render进行生成式立体声渲染以增强声学细节。训练策略包括质量感知预训练课程、监督初始化、离线DPO和在线GSPO的渐进式后训练。

Result: 在600个中英文提示词上，Qwen-Music在16项客观音乐性和音频质量指标中13项达到SOTA。专业评估者对Qwen-Music的偏好度超过领先商业系统。在翻唱任务中，Qwen-Music比领先商业系统更准确地保留参考旋律。

Conclusion: Qwen-Music通过创新的Melody-CoT机制、三组件架构和精细的多阶段训练策略，在文本到音乐生成和翻唱歌曲生成两个任务上均达到了领先水平，证明了其作为强大音乐生成模型的有效性。

Abstract: In this report, we introduce Qwen-Music, a powerful music generation model capable of producing highly musical and high-fidelity songs with complete vocal singing. Qwen-Music supports two core tasks: Text to Music Generation, which create entirely new songs from text descriptions, lyrics, and musical attributes, and Cover Song Generation, which reinterprets existing songs with different styles and vocal characteristics. Architecturally, Qwen-Music integrates three core components: Qwen-Music-Tokenizer, Qwen-Music-LLM, and Qwen-Music-Render. Qwen-Music-Tokenizer compresses audio into a 25 Hz single-codebook stream of Music Semantic Tokens that preserve semantic and melodic information for LLM prediction. Based on these tokens, Qwen-Music-LLM performs autoregressive music semantic modeling, with a key novelty being a melody-token-based chain-of-thought (Melody-CoT) mechanism that plans melodies before full-song generation, improving creativity, musicality, structural coherence, and reference-audio-based melody cloning. To overcome the fidelity limitations of discrete semantic tokens, Qwen-Music-Render performs generative stereo rendering, enriching acoustic details and producing high-fidelity stereo waveforms. Finally, we train Qwen-Music-LLM on more than 5 million hours of multilingual music data covering hundreds of languages. We first apply quality-aware pre-training curriculum, then use progressive post-training, comprising supervised initialization, offline DPO, and online GSPO, to further improve musicality and instruction-following ability. Across 600 Chinese and English prompts, Qwen-Music achieves state-of-the-art results in 13 of 16 objective musicality and audio-quality metrics. Professional evaluators also prefer Qwen-Music over leading proprietary systems. For cover song generation, Qwen-Music preserves reference melodies more accurately than leading proprietary systems.

### [143] [VoxENES 2026: Benchmarking Generalization of Speech Spoofing Detectors Against LLM-Era TTS and Voice Conversion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11706)
*Aastha Sharma,Guangjing Wang*

Main category: cs.SD

TL;DR: 论文提出了VoxENES 2026基准，包含53,628个由10种现代语音合成方法生成的英西双语音频样本，在10种标准化后处理条件下评估了8个预训练检测器，发现最佳模型EER仅28.98%，多数检测器性能接近或低于随机水平，揭示了现有检测器对脆弱伪影的依赖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代LLM驱动的TTS和VC系统生成的合成语音与旧有欺骗基准中的生成器存在差异，导致时间泛化差距，使得检测器在真实后处理条件下的鲁棒性被高估。

Method: 构建VoxENES 2026双语基准（英语和西班牙语），包含53,628个样本，使用10种当代语音合成方法生成，并在10种标准化后处理条件下评估8个预训练检测器（无微调）。

Result: 最佳模型整体EER为28.98%，多数检测器在现代生成器和扰动下性能接近或低于随机水平。

Conclusion: 当前检测器严重依赖脆弱的伪影特征，VoxENES 2026可作为开发鲁棒音频欺骗对抗措施的有效测试平台。

Abstract: Modern LLM-driven text-to-speech (TTS) and voice conversion (VC) systems produce synthetic speech that differs from the generators represented in many legacy spoofing benchmarks. This mismatch creates a temporal generalization gap that can overestimate detector robustness under real-world post-processing conditions. We bridge this gap by introducing VoxENES 2026, a bilingual (English and Spanish) benchmark of 53,628 audio samples generated using 10 contemporary speech synthesis methods and evaluated under 10 standardized post-processing conditions. Using VoxENES 2026, we benchmark eight pretrained detectors without fine-tuning and observe substantial performance degradation: the best model achieves 28.98\% EER overall, while most perform near or below random chance across modern generators and perturbations. Our results highlight the reliance on brittle artifacts in current detectors and establish VoxENES 2026 as a practical testbed for developing robust audio spoofing countermeasures.

### [144] [Encoder-Side Neuron Identification and Amplification for Acoustic Perception in Large Audio-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11801)
*Yu-Han Huang,Chih-Kai Yang,Ke-Han Lu,An-Yu Cheng,Hung-yi Lee*

Main category: cs.SD

TL;DR: 本文提出IAAN方法，通过识别和放大音频编码器中的声学神经元（无需训练或标签），在推理时显著提升大型音频语言模型对非语义语音属性（如情感）的感知能力，在三个模型上平均准确率提升9.7-25.7个百分点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型音频语言模型在语音内容理解上表现优异，但对细粒度、非语义属性（如说话人情绪）感知不足。现有推理时干预方法仅在编码器之后操作且粒度较粗，未探索编码器内部神经元级别的干预，因此需要一种无需重训练、可在推理时有效增强声学感知的方法。

Method: IAAN方法通过对比真实波形与噪声参考上每个前馈神经元的激活值，计算声学得分，识别对真实声学信息敏感的神经元，然后在推理时放大得分最高的少量神经元。该方法无需训练、无需标签，仅在音频编码器内部进行。

Result: 在10种非语义语音属性上，IAAN使Audio-Flamingo-3平均准确率提升25.7个百分点，Qwen2.5-Omni提升21.4，Kimi-Audio提升9.7。即使在已微调优先声学证据的模型上也有提升。编码器位置和神经元级别选择性均被证明是关键因素。

Conclusion: 在音频编码器内部进行小规模、精准的神经元级干预是提升LALM声学理解的有效且未被充分探索的方向，为推理时方法开辟了新路径。

Abstract: Large audio-language models (LALMs) often underperform on fine-grained, non-semantic attributes of speech, such as a speaker's emotion, despite strong performance on speech content. Improving this without the cost of retraining calls for an effective inference-time intervention, yet most existing methods intervene only after the audio encoder and operate at a relatively coarse granularity. The encoder itself, where acoustic information is first extracted from the waveform, remains largely unexplored, especially at the level of individual neurons. We introduce IAAN, Identifying and Amplifying Acoustic Neurons, a training-free and label-free method that scores each feed-forward neuron in the audio encoder by contrasting its activation on the real waveform with that on a noise reference lacking the real audio's acoustic information. IAAN then amplifies a small set of the highest-scoring neurons at inference. Across ten non-semantic speech attributes, IAAN improves average accuracy by 25.7 points on Audio-Flamingo-3, 21.4 on Qwen2.5-Omni, and 9.7 on Kimi-Audio. It also improves a model already explicitly fine-tuned to prioritize acoustic evidence. In controlled comparisons, both the encoder locus and neuron-level selectivity prove necessary for this gain. Intervening after the encoder, at the decoding side or inside the language model, yields little to no improvement, or even deteriorates accuracy. The improvement also depends on which specific neurons are amplified, not merely on their number, confirming that IAAN's acoustic score succeeds in identifying the neurons that matter. These results show that a small, precisely targeted intervention inside the audio encoder is an effective and largely untapped way to strengthen the acoustic understanding of LALMs, opening a new direction for inference-time methods that improve acoustic perception through neuron-level access to the encoder.

</details>

### [145] [Loop-type geometric folding of exact solutions of shifted nonlocal NLS and MKdV equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10870)
*Aslı Pekcan*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文基于折叠子（foldon）概念，提出了一种几何框架，用于构建移位非局部非线性薛定谔方程和修正Korteweg-de Vries方程的折叠参数化波表示。通过非单调参数化空间坐标，利用一孤子和二孤子解生成不同类型的环状折叠轮廓，并分析了变形参数和求解参数对折叠波几何结构的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的(2+1)维可积模型中构造环的方法依赖于通用变量分离方法或hodograph变换，作者希望提出一种更简化的几何方法，将折叠结构引入(1+1)维移位非局部方程中。

Method: 基于折叠子概念，采用空间坐标的非单调参数化方法，给出折叠发生的充分条件（折叠映射导数的符号变化），并应用一孤子和二孤子解生成不同折叠轮廓。

Result: 不同的折叠映射生成不同类型的环状折叠轮廓，包括规则环状、振荡型和奇异型折叠轮廓；折叠效应仅改变空间参数化，而不影响解本身；变形参数和求解参数显著影响折叠波的几何结构。

Conclusion: 该几何框架为构造移位非局部非线性波方程的折叠波解提供了一种简洁有效的方法，揭示了折叠现象本质上是一种空间参数化的修正。

Abstract: Based on the notion of foldon, we introduce a geometric framework for constructing folded parametric wave representations of exact solutions of some shifted nonlocal nonlinear Schrödinger and modified Korteweg-de Vries equations. Unlike the method of constructing loops in $(2+1)$-dimensional integrable models based on universal variable separation approach or hodograph transformation, we consider a simplified geometric approach of constructing loop-type folded profiles via non-monotonic parametrization of the spatial coordinate associated with the exact solution of the $(1+1)$-dimensional shifted nonlocal equations. A sufficient condition under which folding takes place is provided in the form of sign change of the derivative of folding map. Applying one- and two-soliton solutions of various shifted nonlocal nonlinear Schrödinger and modified Korteweg-de Vries equations found earlier, we show how different folding maps generate different loop-type folded profiles. In particular, we analyze the influence of deformation parameters and solution parameters on the geometry of folded waves. We show that the effect of the folding leads only to the modification of the spatial parametrization and generates various geometric structures like regular loop-type, oscillating-type, and singular-type folded profiles for certain values of parameters.

</details>

### [146] [WaveNet-Style Guitar Amplifier Model Pruning for Real-Time iOS Deployment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10086)
*Ryota Sato,Eli Silverstein*

Main category: eess.AS

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于稀疏化WaveNet的iOS推理引擎，通过90%权重剪枝和自定义稀疏C++引擎，在iPhone CPU上实现低延迟实时神经网络吉他放大器模拟，音质无损且匹配原模型至int16量化误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: WaveNet风格的卷积网络能以高保真度模拟电子管放大器和失真效果器，但其计算开销过大，导致模型只能运行在桌面端或专用DSP硬件上，无法在移动设备上实时运行。

Method: 采用迭代幅度剪枝（Iterative Magnitude Pruning）去除90%网络权重，并构建自定义稀疏C++推理引擎，将稀疏性直接转化为计算加速，在仅使用CPU的iPhone上实现低延迟实时推理。

Result: 剪枝后模型在iPhone CPU上实现低延迟实时运行（稠密模型无法做到），输出与训练模型匹配至int16量化误差级别，且音质无感知损失。

Conclusion: 通过极大幅度的结构化剪枝与定制化稀疏引擎，成功将神经网络吉他放大器模型部署到移动端实时场景，验证了深度稀疏化在音频效果建模中的可行性与实用性。

Abstract: WaveNet-style convolutional networks emulate tube amplifiers and distortion pedals with high fidelity, but their computational cost has confined them to desktops or dedicated DSP hardware. We present a sparse-enabled WaveNet inference engine for iOS that runs heavily pruned neural guitar amplifier models in real time on iPhones. Aggressive iterative magnitude pruning removes 90% of the network weights with no perceptible loss in quality. A custom sparse C++ engine turns this sparsity directly into compute savings, sustaining low-latency real-time operation on a CPU-only iPhone implementation where the dense model cannot. On-device output matches the trained model to within int16 quantization error. At the demonstration, visitors will play a guitar through the app on iPhone hardware and A/B the on-device pruned model against the physical pedal it emulates. Source code and audio examples are available at https://github.com/ryos17/wavenet-imp.

</details>


### [147] [CoFi-Lite: Pushing the Limits of Ultra-Lightweight Speech Enhancement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10142)
*Leyan Yang,Dahan Wang,Xiaobin Rong,Jiadong Zhao,Jing Lu*

Main category: eess.AS

TL;DR: 本文提出CoFi-Lite，一种用于语音增强的超轻量模型，通过粗-细粒度双流解耦的谱建模和跨路径融合模块，以极低计算量（12.87M MACs/s，83.12k参数） outperforms 基线GTCRN（仅需其40.26%计算量），扩展版本性能与SOTA模型AdaptCRN相当且计算成本降低19.34%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 边缘设备上部署深度学习语音增强算法需要超轻量模型，现有方法虽已取得计算复杂度与性能的平衡，但进一步降低复杂度需要更精巧的设计。

Method: 提出CoFi-Lite，将谱建模解耦为粗粒度（全带包络）和细粒度（低频细节）两个并行对称的编码器-解码器路径，并引入Cross-Path Fusion (CPF)模块实现跨路径特征交互。

Result: CoFi-Lite仅需12.87M MACs/s和83.12k参数；性能优于超轻量基线GTCRN，计算量仅为其40.26%；扩展版本性能与SOTA模型AdaptCRN相当，计算成本降低19.34%。

Conclusion: CoFi-Lite通过粗-细粒度双流解耦和跨路径融合的设计，在极低计算资源下实现了优异的语音增强性能，为边缘设备部署提供了高效方案。

Abstract: Ultra-lightweight models are essential for the deployment of deep learning-based speech enhancement algorithms on edge devices. Although recent approaches have achieved a certain balance between computational complexity and performance, pushing the complexity limits further demands more sophisticated designs. In this letter, we propose CoFi-Lite, a highly efficient model that decouples spectral modeling into coarse- and fine-grained streams. By leveraging two parallel and symmetric encoder-decoder paths, it simultaneously extracts full-band envelopes and low-frequency details for complementary enhancement. In addition, a novel Cross-Path Fusion (CPF) module is introduced to bridge the distinct paths, facilitating efficient feature interaction. Remarkably, CoFi-Lite requires extremely low computational resources, featuring only 12.87M MACs/s and 83.12k parameters. Experimental results demonstrate that our proposed model outperforms the ultra-lightweight baseline GTCRN while requiring only 40.26% of its computational complexity. Its scaled-up variant also delivers performance on par with that of the SOTA ultra-lightweight model AdaptCRN alongside a 19.34% reduction in computational cost. Audio examples are available at https://acceleration123.github.io/CoFiLite-demo/.

</details>


### [148] [Evaluating SSL and ViViT Architectures for Cross-Corpus Audio MOS Prediction via LODO Validation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10146)
*Mustafa Ozan Duman,Ahmet Emir Dirik*

Main category: eess.AS

TL;DR: 本研究对三种架构（冻结自监督学习、微调自监督学习、视频视觉Transformer）在自动平均意见分预测任务上进行综合基准测试，采用留一数据集出协议评估域迁移鲁棒性。结果表明：纯英文语料库提升所有架构的预测精度；微调自监督学习在可见数据上性能最佳，但冻结自监督学习在未见分布上表现出更优鲁棒性（URGENT 2024基准MSE 0.36，接近领域优化SOTA的0.30）；视频视觉Transformer在纯英文试验中表现稳定但整体能力低于自监督模型。最优英文仅自监督-Transformer模型已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动平均意见分预测对大规模合成语音和音频增强系统的评估至关重要，但现有模型常面临域迁移问题，即训练数据与测试数据分布不一致导致性能下降。因此需要系统性评估不同架构在跨域场景下的泛化能力，以找到既精准又鲁棒的解决方案。

Method: 采用三阶段评估：（1）构建包含19个数据集、13万样本的综合语料库及17数据集的纯英文语料库；（2）使用留一数据集出协议系统量化可见分布与未见分布之间的泛化差距；（3）通过ARECHO框架将最优模型与18个SOTA指标进行对比。对比三种架构：冻结自监督学习、微调自监督学习和视频视觉Transformer。

Result: 纯英文语料库在所有架构上均提升预测精度；微调自监督学习在可见验证数据上性能最高，但冻结自监督学习在未见分布上鲁棒性更优（URGENT 2024基准MSE 0.36，接近SOTA的0.30）；视频视觉Transformer在纯英文试验中表现稳定但整体低于自监督模型；留一数据集出结果确认模型在可见样本上显著优于未见样本。

Conclusion: 冻结自监督学习嵌入结合深度Transformer编码器为通用语音质量评估提供了最稳定且可扩展的解决方案，最优英文仅自监督-Transformer模型及权重已在Hugging Face开源以支持后续研究。

Abstract: Automatic Mean Opinion Score (MOS) prediction is essential for evaluating large-scale synthetic speech and audio enhancement systems, yet models frequently struggle with domain shift. This study presents a comprehensive benchmarking of three architectural frameworks: Frozen Self-Supervised Learning (SSL-FRZ), Fine-Tuned SSL (SSL-FT), and a Video Vision Transformer (ViViT). Evaluation is conducted in two phases: Part I utilizes a consolidated corpus of 130,000 samples across 19 diverse datasets, while Part II focuses on a purified 17-dataset English-only corpus. To assess robustness, a systematic Leave-One-Dataset-Out (LODO) protocol is employed to quantify the generalization gap between seen and unseen distributions. Finally, the top-performing model is benchmarked against 18 state-of-the-art (SOTA) metrics using the ARECHO framework. Results demonstrate that an English-only purified corpus consistently yields higher predictive precision across all architectures. While SSL-FT achieves the highest performance on seen validation data, the SSL-FRZ model provides superior robustness on unseen distributions, achieving a competitive Mean Squared Error (MSE) of 0.36 on the URGENT 2024 benchmark-closely matching domain-optimized SOTA metrics (MSE 0.30). Although the ViViT architecture remains below SSL-based models in total capacity, it delivers stable results in English-only trials. LODO results confirm that while models perform significantly better on seen samples, frozen SSL embeddings combined with deep Transformer encoders offer the most stable and scalable solution for universal speech quality assessment. To support further research, the top-performing English-only SSL-Transformer model and weights are made publicly available via Hugging Face.

### [149] [Hearing Like Humans? Sound Symbolism and Perceptual Alignment in Speech Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10162)
*Yun-Shao Tsai,Chun-Wei Chen,Chee-En Yu,Yi-Cheng Lin,Hung-yi Lee*

Main category: eess.AS

TL;DR: 本研究首次使用真实语音录音探究语音语言模型（SLMs）是否具备声音象征（sound symbolism）倾向，发现SLMs在听觉判断上与人类感知严重不符，无法捕捉驱动人类直觉的声学线索（如频谱倾斜），且开源模型无法可靠地将听到的声音与对应形状关联。通过视觉对照实验，确认缺陷定位在语音表征层面，而非视觉能力不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前对语音语言模型是否具有声音象征倾向的评估依赖于文本或图像，而非真实语音，因此这一问题尚未得到充分研究。

Method: 使用真实人类语音录音，分别在听觉、跨模态和视觉三个维度上比较模型判断与人类数据，并通过纯视觉对照实验排除形状感知能力的干扰。

Result: SLMs的听觉判断与人类感知一致性差，无法捕捉频谱倾斜等关键声学线索；开源模型无法可靠地将语音与其对应的形状进行跨模态关联；缺陷根源在于语音表征方式，而非视觉能力。

Conclusion: 实现感知对齐的关键不在于更强的视觉能力，而在于能够捕捉人类所听到的声学线索的语音表征。

Abstract: Sound symbolism, the human tendency to map speech sounds to perceptual qualities such as roundness or sharpness, arises primarily from the acoustics of speech rather than spelling. Whether Speech Language Models (SLMs) share this tendency remains open, as prior evaluations rely on text or images rather than real speech. We study it using genuine human speech recordings, comparing model judgments against human data across the auditory, crossmodal, and visual components of the effect. We find that SLMs' auditory judgments align poorly with human perception and miss the acoustic cues, such as spectral tilt, that drive human intuitions, and open-weight models cannot reliably link a heard sound to its corresponding shape. With a visual-only control ruling out shape perception, the weakness localizes to how speech is represented, suggesting that perceptual alignment depends not on stronger vision but on speech representations that capture the cues humans hear.

</details>

Method: 采用双耳听感实验，使用录制电动车经过声音作为刺激材料，呈现包含单车和多车在内的不同交通场景；选定刺激在空间上排列模拟车辆从相反方向接近；让参与者在每次刺激后评价烦扰感知，比较单车与多车AVAS声音场景下的烦扰反应。

Result: 多辆电动车AVAS声音同时存在时，其烦扰感知与单车呈现时存在差异；不同重叠程度的AVAS声音对烦扰感知有不同影响。

Conclusion: 电动车AVAS声音研究应从传统的孤立声源视角转向场景化视角，以更真实地反映实际交通环境中的声音感知体验。

Abstract: The increasing usage of electric vehicles in urban environments has resulted in a widespread presence of AVAS sounds. While individual vehicle sound design and testing is a common approach, real-world traffic scenarios often involve the simultaneous presence of multiple vehicles. Their combined presence may lead to changes in perception, compared to when they are presented individually, specifically regarding annoyance. The work addresses annoyance perception in scenarios involving multiple electric vehicle AVAS sounds. It changes the traditional isolated source-based view into a scene-based one by investigating the combined presence of multiple vehicle sounds as they are experienced in realistic traffic environments. Binaural listening tests were conducted using recorded electric vehicle pass-by sounds. The stimuli presented different traffic scenarios, including single and multiple-vehicles. Selected stimuli were spatially arranged to simulate vehicles approaching from opposite directions. After each stimulus, participants rated their perceived annoyance, enabling a comparison of annoyance responses between isolated and multiple AVAS sound scenarios. The test investigated how different levels of overlapping AVAS sounds affect perceived annoyance when multiple electric vehicles are passing by.

### [153] [FdAudio: MeanFlow-Anchored Fréchet-Distance Post-Training for One-Step Text-to-Audio Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10421)
*Kuan-Po Huang,Bo-Ru Lu,Ho-Lam Chung,Shih-Hsin Wang,Hung-yi Lee*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有少步采样T2A模型（如MeanAudio）的一步生成质量远低于多步模型，亟需弥合这一差距。

Method: 后训练方法，利用多表示Fréchet距离损失直接优化一步分布；引入MeanFlow一致性目标作为结构锚点，防止多步退化。

Result: FD分数降低11.4%，FAD分数提升28.8%；25步采样路径保持高保真音频合成，匹配或超越强多步模型且计算延迟更低。

Abstract: While recent few-step sampling text-to-audio generation models like MeanAudio substantially accelerate generation by modeling average velocities, their strict one-step generation quality still lags significantly behind multi-step counterparts. We propose FdAudio to bridge this gap. Unlike MeanAudio, which relies solely on regression against target velocity fields, our post-training approach optimizes the final one-step distribution directly across pre-trained embedding spaces via a multi-representation Fréchet-distance (FD) loss. Crucially, to prevent the multi-step degradation that naive post-training with FD-loss causes, we introduce a MeanFlow consistency objective as a structural anchor. Results demonstrate that FdAudio establishes state-of-the-art one-step T2A generation quality among few-step systems, yielding an 11.4% reduction in FD score and a 28.8% improvement in FAD score relative to the baseline MeanAudio framework. Notably, we solve FD post-training's naive multi-step degradation issue by proposing the MeanFlow anchor, enabling a 25-step sampling path to maintain high-fidelity audio synthesis that matches or surpasses strong multi-step models at a fraction of their computational latency.

### [154] [ECHOv2: Two-Level Band-Splitting Representation Learning for Anomalous Sound Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10596)
*Yucong Zhang,Juan Liu,Ming Li*

Main category: eess.AS

TL;DR: ECHOv2是一种用于机器异常声音检测的频带分裂预训练模型，通过带内局部表示学习、带间两级自蒸馏策略和可控制粒度摘要令牌，在DCASE 2020-2025基准上展示了优越性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有预训练音频骨干网络未能充分捕获机器声音的频率特定特性，因此需要一种能够学习细粒度频谱模式并建模跨频率依赖性的鲁棒音频表示方法。

Method: 提出ECHOv2频带分裂模型：1）带内局部表示学习捕获细粒度频谱模式；2）两级自蒸馏策略包含全局上下文对齐和掩码子带重建的显式带间监督；3）引入多个摘要令牌实现结构化聚合和可控频率粒度。

Result: 在DCASE 2020-2025统一ASD基准上，通过嵌入评估（冻结表示判别性）和微调评估（下游迁移性）两种协议验证了有效性，消融实验证实了各组件贡献。

Conclusion: 结构化跨频带建模为ASD表示学习提供了强大且可适应的框架，可作为未来研究的基础。模型和基准均已开源。

Abstract: Machine anomalous sound detection (ASD) requires robust audio representations capable of capturing subtle deviations in machine sounds under limited supervision. Existing pre-trained audio backbones do not fully capture frequency-specific characteristics of machine sounds. To address this, we propose ECHOv2, a band-splitting model that learns localized intra-band representations to capture fine-grained spectral patterns while also incorporating a two-level self-distillation strategy with explicit inter-band supervision to model cross-frequency dependencies. The inter-band branch performs global context alignment and masked sub-band reconstruction, and multiple summary tokens are introduced for structured aggregation with controllable frequency granularity, enabling region-aware interaction across sub-bands during training. This design allows ECHOv2 to robustly handle diverse machine types and noisy operating conditions while maintaining stable representation quality. To enable fair and consistent evaluation of pre-trained audio backbones, we establish a unified ASD benchmark over DCASE 2020-2025 with two complementary protocols: embedding-based evaluation for frozen representation discriminability and adaptation-based evaluation for downstream transferability. Ablation studies confirm the effectiveness of intra-band learning, inter-band supervision, and structured aggregation granularity for robust ASD representation learning. These findings demonstrate that structured cross-band modeling provides a powerful and adaptable framework for ASD representation learning and can serve as a strong foundation for future research. The model and benchmark are fully open-sourced at https://github.com/yucongzh/ECHOv2 and https://github.com/yucongzh/ASD_Benchmark to promote reproducible research.

</details>

Method: 在新建的西班牙语清晰度数据集SpInt上，比较5种参考型指标（STOI, ESTOI, STGI, HASPI, SIIB）与2种深度学习无参考指标（MOSA-Net+, W2V-SIP）的性能，并分析训练-测试声学不匹配的影响。

Result: 参考型OIMs在所有评估场景下均优于无参考指标；无参考深度学习指标在训练-测试声学不匹配（尤其是语言不匹配）时性能显著下降；所有评估指标在开发阶段均未接触过西班牙语数据。

Conclusion: 现有无参考清晰度指标跨语言泛化能力不足，亟需开发更鲁棒和通用的模型；公开SpInt数据集以推动该方向研究。

Abstract: Objective intelligibility metrics (OIMs) enable fast and low-cost evaluation of speech intelligibility and are widely used in speech technology assessment. In this study, we evaluate five reference-based OIMs (STOI, ESTOI, STGI, HASPI, and SIIB) and two deep learning-based no-reference metrics (MOSA-Net+ and W2V-SIP) on SpInt, a new Spanish speech intelligibility dataset. Our results show that reference-based OIMs consistently outperform modern data-driven no-reference approaches, which degrade notably under training-test acoustic mismatches such as language mismatch. This effect is particularly relevant in our scenario, as none of the evaluated metrics were exposed to Spanish speech data during development. Consequently, to foster research on more robust and generalizable no-reference OIMs, SpInt is released publicly.

### [156] [Data Augmentation for L2 English Speaking Assessment using TTS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10790)
*Stefano Bannò,Penny Karanasou,Mengjie Qian,Kate M. Knill,Mark J. F. Gales*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二语口语自动评估依赖大规模标注语音数据，但这类数据相比广泛可用的书面语学习者语料库十分稀缺。为解决这一数据不平衡问题，探索利用TTS和语音克隆将书面二语产出转换为合成语音的可行性。

Method: 使用COREFL语料库（同一学习者对同一问题的口语和书面配对回答），首先用大语言模型将书面回答转换为口语风格文本（"口语化"处理），再用TTS/语音克隆模型生成语音；系统分析了基于熟练度、母语等不同说话人-文本配对策略的效果。

Conclusion: 利用TTS和语音克隆将书面二语数据转换为合成口语数据是一种有效的数据增强方法，口语化改写是关键预处理步骤，说话人-文本按熟练度配对效果最优。

Abstract: Automated assessment of second language (L2) speaking proficiency relies on large-scale annotated speech data, which remains scarce compared to widely available written learner corpora. A promising direction for addressing this imbalance is to use text-to-speech (TTS) and voice cloning to convert written L2 production into synthetic speech. However, written and spoken L2 differ fundamentally: spontaneous speech includes disfluencies and discourse markers, while writing is more planned and complex. This raises the question of what is required to generate synthetic L2 speech suitable for assessment. We address this through a systematic analysis of speaker-text relationships using COREFL, a publicly available corpus containing paired spoken and written responses from the same L2 learners to the same questions across modalities. In our proposed framework, we first address the structural differences between written and spoken language by transforming written responses into spoken-style transcripts ("speechification") using a large language model. These transcripts are then converted into speech using a TTS/voice-cloning model. To assign a voice to each synthetic response, we investigate different speaker-text pairing strategies based on shared learner attributes (proficiency level, first language, both, or neither). We evaluate our data augmentation techniques on the language assessment task, with improvements shown in both wav2vec2 (audio-based) and ModernBERT (text-based) scoring systems. Results show that matching speakers and texts by proficiency level yields the most robust synthetic speech. Moreover, raw written text leads to a strong mismatch with spoken language, while speechification substantially reduces this gap and improves grading performance.

### [157] [Tight-Frame Reconstruction for Acoustic Intensity Estimation Using Cardioid Microphone Pairs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11059)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统压力差方法对麦克风间距与声波波长关系敏感，且实际心形麦克风偏离理想指向性会产生方向依赖的估计误差，亟需一种鲁棒性更强的声强估计框架。

Method: 采用心形-心形(C-C)方法，基于球形紧框架麦克风配置组合多轴方向性强度分量；使用Legendre多项式和球谐展开表示指向性误差；提出几何依赖的泄漏度量评估误差抑制能力。

Result: 紧框架配置通过几何平均有效抑制方向依赖误差；泄漏度量成功预测了麦克风指向性缺陷对重构声强矢量的影响；在较大麦克风间距下仍能实现准确的宽频带声强估计。

Conclusion: 该框架为使用指向性麦克风阵列进行声强测量提供了一种物理解释性强且实用的方法。

Abstract: This paper investigates acoustic intensity estimation using pairs of cardioid microphones based on the cardioid-cardioid (C-C) method. Unlike conventional pressure-difference techniques, the C-C method is intrinsically less sensitive to the relationship between microphone spacing and acoustic wavelength. However, practical microphones inevitably deviate from ideal cardioid directivity, producing direction-dependent estimation errors.
  To improve robustness against such errors, a measurement framework based on spherical tight-frame microphone configurations is proposed. Directional intensity components measured along multiple axes are combined to reconstruct the three-dimensional acoustic intensity vector. Furthermore, directivity errors are represented using Legendre polynomial and spherical harmonic expansions, and a geometry-dependent leakage metric is introduced to quantify the error-suppression capability of different microphone arrangements.
  Theoretical analysis and numerical simulations demonstrate that tight-frame configurations effectively suppress direction-dependent errors through geometric averaging. The proposed leakage metric successfully predicts the influence of microphone directivity imperfections on the reconstructed intensity vector. The results further indicate that accurate wide-band acoustic-intensity estimation can be achieved even with relatively large microphone spacings, which are generally impractical in conventional pressure-difference approaches. %
The proposed framework provides a physically interpretable and practically useful approach for acoustic intensity measurement using directional microphone arrays.

### [158] [Where Speech Enhancement Hurts Recognition: An Inference Time Polar Projection Diagnosis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11157)
*Mingyue Huo,Yuheng Zhang,Hao Zhang*

Main category: eess.AS

TL;DR: 本文提出极投影（polar projection）方法，用于诊断STFT域语音增强中哪些成分（幅度/相位）损害ASR性能。通过调整幅度强度α和相位修正γ，发现幅度强度是影响ASR的关键轴，相位修正无益。不同ASR模型对幅度修正偏好不同，该方法无需重训练即可缓解增强-识别不匹配问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语音增强能提升感知质量，但未必改善ASR性能。现有解决方法（联合训练、插值等）虽能缓解不匹配，但缺乏对"增强的哪个成分损害识别"的定量诊断和定位。

Method: 提出推理时极投影（polar projection），对STFT域掩模M=Ae^{jφ}构造M_{α,γ}=A^α e^{jγφ}，通过扫描幅度强度α和相位修正γ，在冻结的SE和ASR模型上量化各成分对识别的影响。

Result: 幅度强度是影响ASR的主要维度，相位修正无识别收益。最优幅度强度取决于ASR模型：wav2vec2.0偏好强修正，Whisper偏好弱修正。

Conclusion: 极投影提供了一种无需重训练SE或ASR的简单缓解方法，可直接用于依赖增强语音的语音助手和智能代理。

Abstract: Speech enhancement (SE) can substantially improve perceptual quality, yet enhanced speech does not necessarily improve automatic speech recognition (ASR). Existing remedies, such as retraining the enhancer jointly with recognizer or interpolating enhanced speech with the noisy input, can mitigate this mismatch, but common explanations such as artifacts and over-suppression remain qualitative and do not localize which enhancement component harms recognition. We propose inference time polar projection, a diagnosis for STFT domain enhancement. Given a mask $M=Ae^{jφ}$, polar projection forms $M_{α,γ}=A^αe^{jγφ}$, where $α$ controls magnitude strength and $γ$ controls phase correction. Sweeping these controls on frozen SE and ASR models turns ASR degradation into measurable magnitude and phase effects. Our projection analysis shows that magnitude strength is the operative axis, while estimated phase correction provides no recognition benefit. The optimal magnitude strength is recognizer dependent: waveform-input wav2vec2.0 favors strong correction, whereas log-Mel-input, noise-robust Whisper prefers weaker correction. Finally, the projection provides a simple mitigation for any SE front end in the STFT mask domain, without retraining either the enhancer or the recognizer, making it directly useful for voice assistants and agents that rely on enhanced speech.

</details>


### [159] [Semantic Sampling via Learnable Observation Front Ends](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11260)
*Yuxuan Liu,Guangming Shi,Pengfei He,Shuai Ma,Xiang Cheng*

Main category: eess.AS

TL;DR: 本文提出语义采样（Semantic Sampling），通过可学习的观测前端替代传统低速率波形直接采样。该前端由语义特征滤波器组、约束语义观测矩阵和低速率读出模块组成，将波形映射为多个声学响应通道并组合成少量观测通道，再经重建网络恢复信号。实验表明，在相同观测预算下，该方法的波形保真度、频谱一致性和感知质量均优于传统固定低速率采样和基于预定义波形的神经重建方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统低速率采样主要依据带宽、稀疏性或固定信号级结构从原始波形生成有限维观测，但对于语音等声学信号，与重建相关的信息通常通过内容相关的频谱-时间结构表达，而非仅靠波形采样点。因此需要一种能捕捉语义结构信息的采样方法。

Method: 提出可学习观测前端，包含三个模块：(1) 语义特征滤波器组，将输入波形映射到多个声学响应通道；(2) 约束语义观测矩阵，将多个响应通道组合成少量观测通道；(3) 低速率读出模块，产生低速率有限维样本。其后接重建网络从观测中恢复信号。

Result: 在低速率语音重建实验中，与固定低速率采样和基于预定义波形的神经恢复方法相比，在相同观测预算下，所提语义采样前端能提供更具信息量的观测，在波形保真度、频谱一致性和感知质量上均有提升。

Conclusion: 可学习的观测前端在相同观测预算下能够为声学信号重建保留更多有用信息，验证了语义采样相比传统固定采样策略的优越性。

Abstract: Sampling determines the form of information available to downstream reconstruction systems. Conventional lowrate sampling forms finite-dimensional observations directly from the raw waveform, with the sampling rule mainly guided by bandwidth, sparsity, or fixed signal-level structures. For acoustic signals such as speech, however, reconstruction-relevant information is often expressed through content-related spectral-temporal structures rather than waveform samples alone. This paper proposes semantic sampling via learnable observation front ends, where finite-dimensional observations are generated from learned signal responses instead of directly subsampled waveform points. The proposed front end consists of a semantic feature filterbank, a constrained semantic observation matrix, and a low-rate readout module. The filterbank maps the input waveform into multiple acoustic response channels, the observation matrix combines these responses into a small number of observation channels, and the readout module produces low-rate finite-dimensional samples. A reconstruction network is then used to recover the signal from the resulting observations. Experiments on low-rate speech reconstruction show that, under the same observation budget, the proposed semantic sampling front end provides more informative observations than fixed low-rate sampling and neural restoration methods based on predetermined low-rate waveforms. The improvements in waveform fidelity, spectral consistency, and perceptual quality show that learnable observation front ends preserve more useful information for acoustic signal reconstruction under the same observation budget.

</details>


### [160] [Qwen-Audio-VAE Technical Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11738)
*Ziyue Jiang,Dake Guo,Zekai Zhang,Hangrui Hu,Ting He,Xinfa Zhu,Xiong Wang,Yongqi Wang,Jiapeng Wang,Wenxiang Guo,Zhifang Guo,Chenfei Wu,Dayiheng Liu,Jin Xu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有音频VAE在重建质量与压缩率之间难以兼顾，且编码速度不足以支撑大规模文本到音频训练，亟需一个既能高质量重建多样化音频、又能生成紧凑且快速编码的潜在表示的模型。

Method: 采用因果编码器-解码器结构、窗口Transformer模块和多判别器训练；通过非对称编码器-解码器骨架和延迟感知的编码器剪枝最大化编码吞吐量；在500万小时多领域音频数据上大规模训练。

Conclusion: Qwen-Audio-VAE为高效通用音频生成提供了一个高质量、紧凑且高吞吐量的表示骨干，有效支持大规模文本到音频训练。

Abstract: We introduce \textbf{Qwen-Audio-VAE}, a suite of low-bitrate, fast-encoding continuous audio autoencoders designed for scalable general audio generation. The model is built around a simple but important principle: an audio VAE should not only reconstruct diverse audio with high fidelity, but also produce compact latent representations fast enough to support large-scale text-to-audio training. Qwen-Audio-VAE combines a causal encoder-decoder, window Transformer blocks, and multi-discriminator training to achieve a strong balance between reconstruction quality and compression rate. The model is trained at scale on 5 million hours of multi-domain audio, enabling robust reconstruction across heterogeneous acoustic conditions. To further improve computational efficiency, we adopt an asymmetric encoder-decoder backbone and introduce latency-aware encoder pruning to maximize encoding throughput. Experiments on public speech, music, and sound reconstruction benchmarks show that Qwen-Audio-VAE generalizes well across diverse audio domains and is particularly efficient, requiring only 541 ms to encode 32 minutes of audio. Overall, Qwen-Audio-VAE provides a high-quality, compact, and high-throughput representation backbone for efficient general audio generation.

### [161] [Synchronized Three-Dimensional Vocal-Tract Motion for Speech Synchronization via Joint-Embedding Predictive Architecture Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11772)
*Sheng Li,Takahiro Shinozaki*

Main category: eess.AS

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合生物力学声道模型与神经声码器的语音生成系统，通过JEPA表示学习和RL/CEM轨迹选择实现发音动作与声学载体的对齐，在24词集上取得了8.33% WER和3.174 UTMOS的较好性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代神经语音系统能生成清晰波形但隐藏了发音物理状态，而生物力学声道模型虽能暴露发音结构但直接波形合成不如神经声码器鲁棒，因此需要将两者优势结合。

Method: 采用时长保持的声学载体提供听感波形，经校正的三维声道模型提供同步的颌、唇、舌、软腭、喉部、口腔气流和鼻腔气流运动；通过JEPA风格表示和RL/CEM轨迹选择循环将发音动作与声学载体及物理合理性约束对齐。

Result: 在12组3D录音（24组最小对刺激）上评估：WER 8.33%，CER 4.17%，UTMOS 3.174，平均JEPA得分0.864，平均音色保护得分0.947。

Conclusion: 该方法在保持较好语音识别性能和自然度的同时，成功实现了发音物理状态的显式建模与同步，为可解释语音合成提供了新方向。

Abstract: Modern neural speech systems can generate intelligible waveforms, but they usually hide the physical speech-production state that produced the sound. Conversely, biomechanical vocal-tract models expose articulatory structure, contact behavior, airflow routing, and geometric constraints, but direct physical waveform synthesis remains less robust than modern neural vocoders. A duration-preserving acoustic carrier supplies the listening waveform, while a corrected three-dimensional vocal-tract model supplies synchronized jaw, lip, tongue, velum, laryngeal, oral-airflow, and nasal-airflow motion. A joint-embedding predictive architecture (JEPA)-style representation and a reinforcement learning/cross-entropy method (RL/CEM) trajectory-selection loop align articulatory actions to the acoustic carrier and to physical-plausibility constraints. The evaluation contains 12 3D recordings covering 24 minimal-pair stimuli. On the 24-word set, the carrier obtains good automatic speech recognition (ASR) results (an 8.33\% WER, a 4.17\% CER), a UTMOS score of 3.174, a mean JEPA score of 0.864, and a mean timbre-guard score of 0.947.
